<Review>Up for adventure? Go to the Flumes! This place affords some of the most beautiful Autumn photos you can take in these parts of Northern California. There is a very clear, defined path for walking, and some off-shoots that will take you lower to the river. Bring good shoes though, because there are some perilous falls if you slip. Play it safe and smart, and you'll experience the beauty and wonder of God's glorious world!</Review>< pics>

< Review>
Beautiful area and beautiful walk. Several trails to the river for swimming. I rated it low for 2 reasons. The road down is pretty crazy dirt road. Know your cars limits before you attempt this.  Secondly, the trail seems to be under construction. Several signs say no public access, yet the parking area was full and everyone was ignoring the signs. If you turn right you will eventually come to actual construction and I would not recommend going past.</Review>

<rate>5<//rate>< Text>
A great place for hiking and sight seeing but BEWARE OF THE LAST PART OF THE ROAD LEADING TO THE PARKING SPOT. Its only one lane wide, steep full of super deep potholes and large rocks and very dangerous to drive on. If your car is not in great condition, is low to the ground, or does not have exellent brakes do not attemp this road. I was surprised no one els had warned people in the comments about this road. Its very sketchy! Novice drivers should avoid this road. Maybe park somewhere near the top and walk down? I know I wont be coming back without the truck!</Text>

<text>Zetton on it!  Zetton on it!

Ramen Zetton, the popular Costa Mesa ramen shop, has a new branch nearby me in Cypress.  For their soft opening, Ramen Zetton has priced their ramen bowls from $5 - $7.  Being a ramen lover & not one to pass up a discount, I hurried down to Ramen Zetton, eagerly awaiting slurping up some piping hot ramen.

The traditional ramen condiments are well represented - chili oil, white pepper grinder, vinegar, red chili pepper & house made spicy miso chili paste.

The house made spicy miso chili paste has a definite kick to it.  Not for spice weaklings.

I went for their signature Sesame Miso Tantan ramen ($7, reg. price $8.50)-

The tantan ramen broth is thick, almost curry-like.  Adding the entire jar of spicy miso chili paste, the broth became almost akin to marinara.  Plus, a splash of vinegar, some chili pepper, a drizzling of chili oil, freshly ground white pepper & a splash or 2 of vinegar. The vinegar is what really kicked the flavor profile up a notch.   Hearty & rich, the sesame miso tantan consisted of a special blend of sesame & miso, chicken broth, green onion, ground pork & vegetable puree.  The ramen had a good bite to it.  My preference would've enjoyed them more al dente, but I was not disappointed with the wonderfully thick broth & juicy chunks of ground pork.  At $7, a delicious bowl that's a must get!

Not feeling soup today?  Ramen Zetton's simplistic menu also has various rice dishes & gyoza for your consideration.

Service was good.  I arrived a few minutes before opening.  The father of the owner of Ramen Zetton was running the place.  The cook called in sick & one from the Costa Mesa location was brought in to save the day.  My water was refilled on a couple occasions & I was even given containers of the spicy miso chili paste to take home, w/o asking.  Not a place for large groups, seating is minimal with a few tables, booths & bar seating.

Parking is in private lot.  Hard to spot from the street, Ramen Zetton is located behind Oodles of Noodles Pho Restaurant & adjacent to Poki Roll.

Hurry & get down to Zetton!  Ramen Zetton serves up soothing bowls of ramen that are priced cheaper than their competitors.  The sesame miso tantan ramen was a winner & I'm eagerly anticipating trying their other ramen offerings.  I can't procrastinate, though, as I want to take advantage of Ramen Zetton's soft opening pricing.  Hungry for soup? Check out Ramen Zetton!

Highly recommend!
NOMNOMNOMNOMNOMNOMNOM</text><Pics>None</Pics><resp>None</resp><GmapID>0x80dd2ea7815c0247:0x2a465a172d025a2c<//GmapID></record></dataset><record>

< Text>
Former place for Cambinos and Teriyaki Monkey Wave rises Ramen Zetton. If you've been to this location, you would know how small this kitchen and seating is. I would say it seats about 24-30 people max.  Lots of parking in the lot, near by Icon (For you craft beer people)

As for the Ramen, prices are still discounted for Classic ($5), Old School ($5), Special Salt ($6), Special Soy ($6). Of course, we tried one of each.  The noodles for the $5 are thinner (Chuka-Soba), while the Ramen for the $6 are thicker. The broth for the Classic tasted packaged, the Old school Shoyu had a light soy (my favorite) and the Specials had this Vegetable broth which was a bit too much I thought.

Non of the broth tasted in depth, unlike those day long tonkotsu broths but for what you get, it's okay. The chicken that does come with the noodle tasted like shoyu braised with sugar and that was just okay too. Kitakata is nearby, personally I would go there instead.

Service here with one person is pretty awesome I have to say, even with a packed house.
Yep check in gets you free soda currently.  I will have to make another trip to try the other noodles.<//Text>

We had a fantastic experience. We went on a whale watching tour the morning of Mother's Day. The staff and crew were extremely friendly and helpful. < review>
We had a blast on our whale watching excursion! We had initially reserved a Saturday afternoon tour, but bad traffic from Orange County caused us to show up late and miss the boat. Thankfully, after going to the desk and explaining why we were late, they rebooked us for the Sunday morning tour, no charge. On Sunday morning, we had a fun time on the open sea, and our group saw two individual whales and a massive pod of dolphins. It was incredible seeing hundreds of dolphins (including babies) swimming and jumping alongside the boat. Our tour guide was super knowledgeable and constantly provided interesting facts about the wildlife. The boat was pretty choppy on the way out, and several people in our group got seasick, including my pregnant wife. Luckily they sell motion sickness meds (bodine) for $1 a pill. Bodine (unlike dramamine) is safe for pregnant women to take. All in all, we had a great time, and the wonderful service from the crew made this a 5-star experience.< /review>

< Review>
The trip was nice. I got to see a huge group of dolphins close-up and learned about the correct termini and their interesting behavior. The grey whale at the end of the tour refused to suspend it's dinner for showing up fully at the surface, but the experience was still impressive and the conveyed information about the life of these whales interesting. Right at the start one could see a group of drowsy sea lions and got to know how to tell them apart from seals. A moon fish also passed by. Many sea birds like gulls and pelicans could also be seen closely. Surely you will also have fun.</Review>

<review>If you‚Äôre looking for a spacious boat with a courteous crew, this is the ideal trip to go on. For starters, you‚Äôll find that parking is plentiful and free; couple that with an efficient check-in by professional employees at the landing will leave you satisfied.

The trip itself was great, although the boat was at the end of the dock, it provided a great view of all of other boats at the landing. The crew and captain were very friendly to myself and my girlfriend. The ride was smooth and within 30 seconds we passed a bait barge that held multiple California Sea Lions. It was mentioned that we could possibly see whales within 10-15 minutes of the trip, but did not see anything until roughly 45 minutes in. I was not let down at the size of the humpback whales we saw. Nothing breached significantly, but it was incredible to experience an animal of that size come up to the surface and display itself. To top it off the ocean was calm as glass, with a beautiful view of the San Diego coastline. Simply describing my experience doesn‚Äôt do any justice. I‚Äôd definitely recommend giving this boat a try!<//review>< pictures>

<time>1593530004759</time><rating>5< /rating>< text>
(Translated by Google) On June 28, I participated in whale watching with my family. I am very happy to see some whales and a group of dolphins (about 100-200)!
The whale wasn't close, but I could see the squirting and diving many times. The dolphin was very close. There was also a cute baby dolphin. When looking at dolphins, we recommend the bench outside the first floor rather than the second floor.
I also saw sea lions and seabirds jump vertically into the sea and catch fish near the port.
The boat was clean and slightly swaying, but not terrible, the staff was kind and comfortable.

By the way, if you can not see whales and dolphins, you can board for free the next time, and if you see only dolphins without whales, it will be half price next time.
